The Jisheng Association Reports on Spring Famine in Various Provinces 153

The Shanghai China Jisheng Association, which previously co-organized the winter relief efforts in Shuyang, Jiangsu, with the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, has concluded its work, as detailed in previous reports. A letter was received from the county reporting on the spring famine, stating that the county was severely affected by the breach of the Yellow River south in the first half of the year and had received relief. Although it is now spring, due to excessive rain and snow in winter, the water in the disaster area has not receded, and the victims are crying of hunger and cold, their suffering even worse than before. The current spring relief is a major problem. The county magistrate, witnessing the devastation, cannot sleep in peace, and urgently requests the allocation of relief funds for spring relief. A telegram was also received from Wei Lihuang, the Commander of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Pacification Headquarters, stating that the counties in western Anhui have suffered from disasters and poor harvests for years. Now, in the spring famine, tree bark and grass roots have been almost completely consumed. As farming is about to begin, most of the plowing cattle and seeds are unavailable. Starvation deaths are reported daily, and the desperation has led to banditry, exacerbating the situation. The situation is similar in eastern Hubei and southern Henan. To address the urgent needs, spring relief and seed loans are essential. Lihuang is heartbroken by what he has seen and sends this urgent telegram to plead for the disaster victims. The association is requested to promptly allocate a large sum of relief funds and send personnel to the disaster area for proper management. Furthermore, the Jingning District Party Headquarters and Cheng Zhao Beixi and other townships in Zhejiang Province reported disaster due to hailstorms, destroying late rice crops with only 30% harvest. The winter was also marked by continuous rain and snow for months, with no clear skies. The county's main food source, sweet potato, was completely ruined by mold. Most farmers are hungry and cannot survive. In January and February of this year, the Red Army returned, invading more than ten townships, including Dadi and Jingnan, as well as Sanzhishu Village, only ten miles outside the city, causing widespread disruption. Lamentation fills the air, and there is no way to seek help. They telegraphed requesting the dispatch of personnel to the townships for relief and comfort. The association has determined that the disaster situation in Jiangsu, Anhui, and Zhejiang provinces is severe, with numerous letters and telegrams arriving. The suffering in Sichuan, Henan, and Hubei provinces has been reported in the newspapers. Now is the time of year when food supplies are scarce, and spring famine is pressing. It is hoped that fellow countrymen will contribute generously to save the lives of disaster victims at this critical juncture, and reduce the impact of natural disasters.

Zhabei's Aid to Wang: Council Meeting Due to Hardship Incurred in Public Service 154

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Mr. Wang Binyan of Zhabei received a notice from the Shanghai District Court stating that his residence would be sealed on the 23rd of this month. Upon hearing this news, local public organizations convened an emergency meeting of the Aid Wang Council. Those in attendance included Yin Cunfu, She Xipin, Cai Qiaojun, Li Guangzhen, Chen Weihan, Wang Yiwei, Jiang Zhongliang, Hu Yibo, Wei Zhiqi, Ye Qichang, Xu Zaikang, Qi Bingjun, Ma Rugen, Luo Xingyou, and many other council members. Chairman Yin Cunfu stated that the council has repeatedly petitioned the Jiangsu Provincial Government for the return of funds due to the hardship incurred by Mr. Wang Binyan in public service, as well as asking the Shanghai Municipal Government to provide assistance and the Ministry of Finance to provide relief. The exchange of official documents has been voluminous. Mayor Wu has indeed provided assistance, for which we are deeply grateful. The Ministry of Finance believes that this is a local debt and should be resolved by Jiangsu Province itself. Although the Jiangsu Provincial Government acknowledges it as a provincial debt, it has no funds to allocate at the moment and suggests that the national treasury should first repay a portion. Therefore, the matter remains unresolved. At the last meeting, all the circumstances were presented to the Executive Yuan for an appeal, but there has been no response yet. Unexpectedly, the court, due to the lawsuit filed by the creditor Guangdong Bank, has no choice but to seal his private property tomorrow. From then on, Mr. Wang's residence will have to be auctioned off to repay the debt, leaving him with no place to live. This is truly heartbreaking. This loan was originally used to cover urgent military expenses. In order to meet the urgent need, he temporarily mortgaged his private residence. The council members were all those who provided funds at the time and should be aware of this. Mr. Wang has suffered for the public good, and there is no way to redress the grievance. Although Shanghai gentry and businessmen Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yiting, Lin Kanghou, Chen Aishi, Zhang Xiaolin, and Shen Lianfang have repeatedly telegraphed the provincial government and the Ministry of Finance, requesting the allocation of 84,000 yuan to settle the personal debt and end the lawsuit, it has been unsuccessful. We are deeply grateful for their enthusiastic assistance. However, once the property is sealed, Mr. Wang will suffer even more. What measures should we take to provide assistance? Chen Weihan, Xu Zaikang, and others spoke in succession, discussing two possible solutions: First, we should send representatives to negotiate with the creditor to request a temporary suspension of the lawsuit, pending the Executive Yuan's approval, which will provide a solution. We should also go to Tongdeli to request a delay in the sealing and submit it to the court for verification. We should also ask Mr. Du Yuesheng for assistance. This was unanimously approved. Second, we should telegram Premier Jiang of the Executive Yuan, requesting relief. The Ministry of Finance should temporarily advance 84,000 yuan to settle the lawsuit and personal debts, and then order the provincial government to settle the real estate and all debts. We should also telegraph the provincial government and the Ministry of Finance again, requesting that they present the circumstances to the Executive Yuan, proving the facts. Representatives should be sent to meet with President Cai Yuanpei and Mr. Chen Aishi and Mr. Zhang Yueli, explaining Mr. Wang's situation and the various ways he has served the government, requesting assistance. This was unanimously approved. The meeting was adjourned.

Russian Guard on Shengjing Ship Kicks Chinese Worker to Death 162

Brutal Attack Without Reason

Russian Arrested and Detained Awaiting Punishment

The Taikoo Company's Shengjing ship had returned to Shanghai from Tianjin after loading cargo. Before the unloading was completed, at 6:40 PM in the evening, a dockworker named A Fu (from Zhenjiang), accompanied by his companion Zhang Maoshun (from Ningbo), boarded the ship to check how much cargo remained. A Russian guard named Kexin (transliteration), saw them and went to drive them away. A Fu and Zhang knew they could not reason with him and started to walk back to the dock and had just stepped onto the ladder when the guard kicked Zhang Maoshun, who was at the back, five times in the lower body with his leather shoe. He then turned around and kicked A Fu in the lower body, injuring him. A Fu immediately fell to the ground, unconscious. His companion helped A Fu onto the dock and was preparing to send him to the hospital, but A Fu died within half an hour. The Water Police Station learned of the incident. Considering it a case of homicide, they immediately dispatched a detective to board the ship and take the Russian guard Kexin into custody. Yesterday morning, Detective Cheng Yongnian submitted a report to the District Court, requesting an inquest and asking that the Russian be taken into custody for investigation. Chief Judge Zhong immediately prepared a document, dispatched police to accompany Detective Cheng to the British Consulate to sign it, and then brought the Russian back to the court. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu filed the case for investigation. As a result, he ordered the suspect to be detained pending further instructions. Prosecutor Liu Shiqing and Investigator Shen Qixiu arrived on the scene to conduct an inquest.

Moon Closest to Earth: Huangpu River High Tide Yesterday 163

Morning and Afternoon Tides Both Over Ten Feet High

Rarely Seen During Spring High Tides

Yesterday, due to the moon being closest to the Earth and it being the first day of the lunar month, the tide in the Huangpu River was unusually high. The morning tide abruptly began at 0:55 AM yesterday morning, reaching 10 feet 1.8 inches. Subsequently, the high tide rose again at 1:00 PM, reaching 10 feet 0.9 inches. It began to recede after 3:00 PM. The high tide was rarely seen during the spring high tides. However, due to clear weather and the upstream of the Yangtze River being in a dry season, the predicted height was not exceeded, but the tide occurred rapidly, and the water flow was extremely turbulent.

Old Prisoner Extorts New Inmate 165

New Inmate Should Not Have Been Beaten by the Group

Two Front Teeth Were Knocked Out

Yang Jinkui, a 40-year-old man from Anhui who had previously been a clerical worker, was sentenced to three years in prison by the Second Special Court on December 18, 1933, for theft. He was released on parole from the Second Special District Prison on October 27 of last year. On the 4th of this month, he was detained by the Public Concession police on suspicion of pickpocketing on a tram and brought to the First Special Court. He was found not guilty due to lack of evidence. However, a parole certificate from the Second Special Court was found on Yang, so he was sent to the French Concession police station. On the 21st, he was handed over to the Second Special Court. Lawyer Yuan Jiahuang of the police station stated that the defendant's address after parole did not match his current address, which was a violation of parole regulations. Yang argued that his residence was not in violation, and the theft in the British Concession was only a suspicion. He pleaded for investigation, stating that he was engaged in honest business and dared not violate the law. Judge Wang Gangxu reviewed the testimony and ordered Yang to be temporarily detained pending execution and that his guarantor be brought in to take him away. Thus, Yang Jinkui was temporarily detained in the Special Four room of the Second Special Court detention center. To everyone's surprise, prisoners Dong Afu (a 30-year-old Ningbo man sentenced to two and a half years for theft) and Sun Azhong (a 30-year-old Ningbo man sentenced to two and a half years for theft), who were responsible for cleaning duties in the detention center (referred to as "small chains"), saw that Yang was well-dressed and believed he was a wealthy detainee. They attempted to extort money from him unsuccessfully. On the 22nd (Sunday), they led more than ten other detainees in beating Yang, causing him to fall to the ground unconscious. The warden learned of the incident and went to the scene, causing the perpetrators to scatter. Yang Jinkui identified Dong and Sun as the ringleaders. The warden reported the incident to the Second Special Court Procuratorate. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Prosecutor Wang Ren and a clerk went to the Fifth Court to investigate. Yang Jinkui testified that on Saturday of last week, he was temporarily detained in the Special Four room of the detention center, where a "small chain" (Dong Afu) told him to be sensible and asked if he understood the rules. He was told to write a note to his family to send money to treat the others (referred to as "running a note"). When he refused, Dong slapped him twice. Yesterday, he was moved to Special One, told to sit in the toilet, and then a group arrived, covered his face with a handkerchief, and threw him to the ground with force (referred to as "pushing the mountain and overturning the earth"). He lost consciousness and two of his front teeth were knocked out. He could not identify the other assailants. One of the guards, Zhao Qusheng, knew in advance that they were going to beat him, but not only did he not stop them, he said, "Wait until after he's off duty, then you can beat him." Officer Zhao Qusheng was summoned and asked if he knew in advance that they were going to fight. He replied that he did not. He was asked why they were fighting. He replied that it was because Yang was blocking the way when the "small chain" was taking the rice bucket out to get food, and Yang refused to move, so they argued. Dong Afu testified that it was because Yang was obstructing traffic and argued with the inmates. He denied leading a group to attack him or attempting to extort money. Sun Azhong testified that Yang and Dong argued, and he went forward to mediate, but he did not help with the assault or attempt to extort money. At this point, Prosecutor Wang told Yang Jinkui that he could request the warden to file a criminal self-accusation with the court. Dong and Sun were returned to the detention center. Yang Yugui was sent to the court for examination of his injuries.

Korean Kim Youshan Forcibly Sends Wife to Asylum 166

Wife is Chinese, Gains Husband's Displeasure, Falsely Accused of Mental Illness

Asylum Doctors and Others Reported by Police Station and Sued in Court

The Shanghai Mental Hospital, located at 7 Chunjiang Villa, Lane 888, Kangning Road, Shanghai, has been open for several years. The director is Gu Wenjun. Recently, doctors from the hospital, Chu Jiqun, male nurse Gao Xinkui, tea server Yang Caigou and Li Amao were criminally sued in the First Special District Court by the Gordon Road Police Station for illegally detaining a Tianjin woman, Pan Jingwen, from February 12th, 10 AM to the 13th, depriving her of freedom of movement, violating Article 302 of the Criminal Law on obstructing freedom, and assaulting her, violating Article 277 of the Criminal Law on injury. The Special Court issued summons yesterday morning, ordering detectives Lu Gendi and the Western Detective Chief Tuile to summon Chu Jiqun and the other three people to the Eighth Criminal Court. Judge Liu Guisheng took the seat for the trial. The victim, Pan Jingwen, hired a lawyer to attach a civil lawsuit, seeking damages of 1,488.40 yuan. The defendants also hired three lawyers to defend them. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the police station began by detailing the case, stating that the victim, Pan Jingwen, had been at 913 Haining Road.

Hongkou Obstetrics 167

The hospital's student member, Ms. Yu, married Mr. Jin Youshan, a Korean manager of the Jin Tuo Shuibi (Golden Camel Fountain Pen) Factory at 228 Changping Road on November 1st last year, and published a notice in the newspaper. After the marriage, they cohabited at 7 Lane 702 Gordon Road. Unexpectedly, within a few days, a rift developed between the couple. It turned out that a 19-year-old woman named Wang Jifang, a colleague of Ms. Pan, was beautiful. She often accompanied Pan Jingwen home to play, which led to Jin Youshan falling in love with her, viewing Ms. Pan as a thorn in his side. As a result, the rift arose, her treatment gradually deteriorated, and beatings followed. On February 12th of this year, they even claimed that Ms. Pan had a mental illness. Jin, along with defendants Gao Xinkui, Yang Caigou, Li Amao, as well as Gao Shizhong and two Japanese men, Mu Ling, had Pan's hands tied behind her back, hired a car, and forcibly sent her to the Shanghai Mental Hospital. After entering the hospital, they forcibly sat Ms. Pan on a chair in the courtyard, tied her hands and feet, forced her to take medicine, poured cold water on her, stripped off her clothes, and sent her to a small room upstairs, where she was locked away. At that time, Pan Jingwen, believing that she had no mental illness and that the hospital was not using proper methods of treatment but only unreasonable violence, refused to eat out of anger. The defendants then beat her with a leather whip and prohibited her from moving freely. Jin Youshan had prepaid Ms. Pan's room and board for one month, intending to imprison his wife for a long time. Unexpectedly, a maid named Niu Wangshi, who worked for Jin, witnessed her mistress being forced into a car and driven away. She immediately reported the incident to Ms. Yang Pan Jingzhi, Ms. Pan's sister. Yang Pan Jingzhi, who worked at the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road, immediately hired a car to the mental hospital upon hearing the news, demanding to see her sister. However, the hospital refused. After repeated requests, she was finally allowed to meet her. Seeing that her sister was covered in injuries, she called Jin Youshan at 7 p.m. on the 13th, and with his permission, transferred Pan Jingwen to the Shanghai Sanatorium for treatment. The injuries healed after three days. After being discharged from the hospital, she reported to the police station. Detective Lu Gendi and Western Detective Tuile first went to the sanatorium to obtain a medical certificate, which stated that Pan Jingwen had injuries on her right and left arms, as well as both legs and waist, with swelling on both sides, but no signs of mental illness, only slight irritation. However, the defendant, Chu Jiqing, claimed that Pan was usually prone to anger and had phlegm blockage. The police went to Jin Youshan's residence at 401, Room 8, 397 Laobazi Road, for investigation. It was confirmed that he was of Goryeo (Korean) nationality. However, Jin claimed that the dispute arose because his wife wanted to seize his authority as the manager of the pen factory, which had happened several times. It was not due to infidelity. The case concerning Jin Youshan will be handled by the Japanese consulate. An investigation revealed that the facilities inside the Shanghai Mental Hospital were not only inadequate in various aspects, but also that the hospital and the defendant, Dr. Chu Jiqing, had not formally registered with the Public Concession Health Department. According to the Public Concession regulations, anyone seeking to admit someone to a mental hospital must first obtain certificates from two doctors to be qualified. The defendants had violated these regulations. The police requested a postponement of the case because they had previously requested Dr. Wei Ligong, a forensic doctor from the court, to investigate the mental hospital, who found that the facilities were incomplete, the patient rooms were rudimentary, and there were already 20 patients inside. When the police returned to investigate a few days ago, eight people were missing. It was claimed that they had all recovered and been discharged. The remaining patients, after examination by Dr. Wei, including male Chen Zhifa, female Zhang Xianyan, and Wang Meiguan, showed no signs of mental illness and were quite lucid. Most of the patients were female, while the doctors and nurses employed by the hospital were all male. Therefore, the police need to investigate further. The victim, Pan Jingwen, claimed to be from Tianjin, 26 years old. On November 1st of last year, she married Jin Youshan through the introduction of Zhang Youfang. She stated that nine days after the marriage, Jin accused her of being old and unable to bear children, wanting to take another concubine. She argued that since the marriage had just begun, how could it be determined that she could not bear children? If she could not bear children in the future, it would not be too late to take a concubine. This led to quarrels and beatings. On the evening of February 11th, she returned home after watching a movie, and Jin, without asking the reason, ordered her to get out. The next day, he, along with the defendants Gao, Yang, and Li, tied her hands behind her back, forced her into a car, and sent her to the mental hospital. At that time, Gao Xinkui claimed to be a detective from Laoxing 136, and upon arriving at the hospital, he was the first to slap her. Yang and Li used leather belts to beat her. Despite her repeated requests, asking them not to misunderstand, explaining that it was just a family dispute, the defendants were aggressive and unreasonable, imprisoning her in a room and pouring cold water on her. In total, she was imprisoned for two days and beaten three or four times. She found that her husband, Jin Youshan, had registered with the Chinese government the year before and had become a Chinese citizen. Furthermore, witnesses Niu Wangshi and Pan Yang Jingzhi filed reports, proving everything. Questioned, Ji Jiqing stated that he and the hospital were both registered. Pan's mother was sent to the hospital by her husband, with a high temper, strong pulse, phlegm blockage, and hitting people, and unclear speech. He diagnosed her with mental illness and prescribed medicine for her. Because she refused to take the medicine, she was tied to a chair and forcibly fed, etc. Gao, Yang, and Li all denied beating her. Judge Liu instructed that the case be postponed for seven days, and all four defendants were allowed to be released on bail, subject to being summoned at any time.

Using Temple Income for Education: Buddhist Association Urges Hubei Provincial Government 168

The Hubei Provincial Government recently proposed using 60% of the income from Buddhist temples to fund education through joint security, causing great panic among the monks, who have called for help, requesting the Chinese Buddhist Association to fight for them according to the law. The Chinese Buddhist Association believes that Buddhist property is already under the supervision of the central government's Regulations for Supervising Temples, and has been repeatedly ordered to be protected by the National Government and the Executive Yuan. The province has suffered from war and floods for years, and the temples are in dire straits, unable to maintain even the Buddhist public welfare and charitable undertakings that have already been established. If they are further exploited, the livelihoods of monks and nuns throughout the province will inevitably be cut off. The Association has decided to make a concerted effort to appeal to the Hubei Provincial Government to consider public opinion and revise the General Outline for Popularizing Education. At the same time, it has telegraphed all temples in the province, urging them to refuse to allocate funds until the case is resolved.

Recent News from the Chinese Numismatic Society 170

The Chinese Numismatic Society has stipulated that a research meeting will be held once a month to exchange and study knowledge of ancient coins. Yesterday (the 22nd) was the date for the society's regular research meeting. More than 20 members, including Wu Zhihui, attended. The research topic was the weight of ancient coins. From the Zhou, Qin, Han, to the Six Dynasties, the weight in *zhu* remained unchanged, with one *liang* equaling 24 *zhu*. The *Han Dabuhuang Qian* weighed one *liang*, and the *Huobu* weighed 25 *zhu*. Based on this, it can be inferred that two *Qin Banliang* were equal to one *Dabuhuang Qian*, five *Han Wushu* were equal to one *Huobu*, four *Sanshu* were equal to one *Qin Banliang*, and each *Bailiang Wushu* weighed eight *zhu*, so three were equal to one *Dabuhuang Qian*, and one was equal to four *zhu*. This continued until the Tang Dynasty, when the system changed greatly. In the early Tang Dynasty, ten *Kaiyuan* coins were equal to one *Tangquan liang*, the same as 60 ancient *zhu*. The people of the Song Dynasty only knew that one *liang* was 24 *zhu*, so they considered each *Kaiyuan* coin to be 2.4 *zhu*, which was a big mistake. In fact, each *Kaiyuan* coin should weigh six *zhu* when measured with an ancient scale. Coin records state that the Song Dynasty scholars' examination of *zhu* was all wrong. The records cited the weights from old documents, which were the system before the Six Dynasties, and were quite valuable. Knowing this and using it to read coin records can prevent one from being misled by the ancients. It is also heard that the society is publishing a journal, and Ding Fubao has been appointed as the editor-in-chief. The collection of manuscripts has begun. Once the organization is complete and approval is obtained for publication, it will be published soon, and it is expected to be famous both at home and abroad.

Longhua Temple Opens 174

Longhua Temple in western Shanghai is a famous ancient temple in Shanghai. It is said to have been built during the Chiwu period (Three Kingdoms era). The temple has a bronze Buddha statue of over 2,000 years old, and the Sutra Depository houses 2,000 volumes of palm-leaf scriptures, but unfortunately, they have been lost, and few remain. The temple is magnificent and very grand. However, it has suffered from repeated wars and is in a dilapidated state. Last spring, the abbot of the temple, Xingkong, renovated it at a cost of 40,000 gold pieces, making it look brand new inside and out. In front of the temple is a seven-story pagoda, next to which is a monument to the soldiers of the 32nd Army who died in battle. Every spring, when the sun shines brightly, and the peach blossoms are red and the willows are green, Longhua Road is crowded with tourists. Recently, due to the warmer weather, the temple was fully opened yesterday for people to visit.

Zheng Yongyu's Appeal Rejected 175

Zheng Yongyu sued Zheng Bozhao for embezzlement and breach of trust. Because he did not accept the first instance judgment of the First Special Court on January 22, he filed an appeal. The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court has now ruled to reject the appeal. The reasons for the judgment are recorded as follows: According to Article 294 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a judgment of dismissal should be pronounced if the statute of limitations for the right to prosecute has expired. After reviewing the original file, the main point of the appellant's lawsuit against Zheng Bozhao for embezzlement and breach of trust lies in attacking Zheng Bozhao for violating his duties and embezzling the Yongtaihe brand name and patent rights before the 28th year (1908 in the Western calendar). Regardless of whether it is calculated according to the seven-year statute of limitations stipulated in Article 69, Paragraph 1 of the old criminal law applicable at that time, or according to the ten-year statute of limitations period stipulated in Article 80, Paragraph 1, Item 2 of the Criminal Law, it has long expired. The original judgment only failed to cite the provisions of Article 2, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. However, its application of the old criminal law Article 69, Paragraph 1, Items 3 and 4, which is most favorable to the actor, considered that the statute of limitations had expired, and pronounced a judgment of dismissal according to the aforementioned provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law. The result is not inappropriate. The appellant's intent is to claim that Yongtaihe is a branch of Yongtai Zhan, and that Zheng Bozhao's use of its brand name and occupation of its profits every day constitutes a continuous act of breach of trust and embezzlement. According to the provisions of Article 80, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, the statute of limitations cannot expire, etc. It is not known that both the crime of embezzlement and breach of trust are both immediate crimes, and the object of the crime of embezzlement only applies to objects and does not include rights. If the embezzlement alleged by the appellant refers to the shop foundation of Yongtai Zhan, then the reorganization of Yongtai Zhan into Yongtaihe was far back in the first year of the Republic of China. Even if Zheng Bozhao had embezzled the shop foundation of Yongtai Zhan, it would have long exceeded the statutory period of extinction. If the embezzlement alleged by the appellant refers to the patent rights for contracting various cigarettes from the British American Tobacco Company, then according to the testimony of Yuse Baise Te, a director of the company, in the original trial, "After I joined the company in 1912, I never knew that Yongtai Zhan had contracted cigarette sales. The contract photo held by the appellant is not a contract for selling the Great Britain brand. Yongtaihe was contracted by Zheng Bozhao, and later changed to a company (in the tenth year of the Republic of China), which he continued to sell." Therefore, even if Yongtai Zhan had contracted cigarette sales for the British American Tobacco Company in the late Qing Dynasty, since the beginning of the Republic of China, its sales rights have long ceased to exist, and there is no continuous or continued embezzlement. As for the breach of trust alleged by the appellant, there are also no specific facts to point to. Moreover, Zheng Bozhao resigned from his position in the seventh year of the Republic of China, which was also admitted by the appellant. Then, calculated from that year, the statute of limitations has also expired. Therefore, the appellant's intent cannot be considered reasonable, no matter from which perspective it is judged. Based on the above conclusion, the judgment should be made according to Article 360 and Article 360 of the Criminal Procedure Law as in the main text.

Maid Dies Tragically from Abortion 178

Xia Zhou, a woman from Huzhou, 36 years old, had been working as a maid for several years at Wu Pinji's sand and gravel business at 6 Tongren Lane, 231 Wuchang Road. Recently, she had a relationship with a certain person and became pregnant for two months. Her abdomen was swollen, which was unseemly. She asked Dai Li, a woman from Gaoyou, to find a way to terminate the pregnancy. Dai introduced her to Li Wu, an old woman from the same hometown, at 38 Zhitong Road, Jiaobei, who agreed to do it for 5 yuan and 5 jiao. Li Wu then inserted a herbal root into Xia Zhou's lower body. However, the surgery was not successful, and she fell ill in bed, moaning in pain. After the hostess noticed, she was sent to Kuangren Hospital for treatment the other day. The treatment was ineffective, and she bled profusely from her lower body and died at 1 a.m. The hospital notified the Hongkou police station, who sent detectives Yang Xianchen and Wang Shubei to the hospital. They transported Xia Zhou's body to the Philun Road mortuary for examination. Dai Li was arrested on Zhitong Road, Jiaobei, but Li Wu had fled after hearing the news. Dai Li was taken to the police station and transferred to the women's prison. Yesterday morning, she was taken to the Criminal Court III of the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Concession, narrated the events in detail and requested a postponement. Questioned, Dai Li's testimony was evasive. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered her to be remanded in custody and postponed the case for further investigation. Zhang Zongru, a prosecutor from the court, arrived at the mortuary to examine Xia Zhou's body and stated that the deceased Xia Zhou, a female, had died as a result of an abortion performed during her lifetime. The body was allowed to be collected by her employer, Wu Pinji, to wait for her family to come to Shanghai to claim it.

To the Editor, According to the legal representative of Siming Bank, upon reading various newspapers, they used large-print headlines to indicate that the Gentai Factory owed rent, and that Cheng Yize was not a shareholder, and had withdrawn part of the case. The content of the articles was all about using our bank's lawsuit to confirm the invalidity of Gentai's withdrawal of the lease and fabricating things out of thin air to benefit Cheng Yize. The intention was to have reporters distribute the articles to various newspapers on the same day, in order to deceive other claim holders and prevent them from listing him as a defendant. However, while our bank withdrew the confirmation lawsuit, it still filed a lawsuit for payment. The list of defendants is the same for both lawsuits, without any changes, including Li Quanshen, the manager of the Gentai Hepen Factory, shareholders Cheng Linsheng and Cheng Yize, and Hu Xiannan, a related party. We request that the two drafts of the lawsuits be sent to the newspapers on our behalf, and urge them to accurately correct the names of the defendants in the letter, so that the truth is not obscured by false statements, and those who fabricate falsehoods will only work harder without success, and the truth can be revealed to all sectors. Therefore, we are urgently writing to your newspaper on behalf of the bank and hope that you will check the precedent for corrections and make the corrections accordingly. To the Shenbao Newspaper, Lawyers Chen Ying and Tang Yan, 25.3.23

Guangdong-Guangxi Industry Inspection Group Report (5) From Yang'an, Wuzhou 186

A Glimpse of Wuzhou, Guangxi's Commercial Center

Wuzhou is located in the east of Guangxi Province, at the meeting point of the Guangxi and Guangdong provinces. It is not only a passage into Guangdong and Hong Kong, but also a distribution center for goods from the three provinces of Guangxi, Guizhou, and Yunnan. Commerce and navigation have always been developed here, making it a hub of commerce in Guangxi Province. However, due to the decline of the rural economy in recent years, it has also been affected by the economic downturn, and commerce has plummeted. The population has decreased from 120,000 to around 80,000. In the 24th year, more than 20 commercial establishments closed down, and the Yongfu Company, jointly operated with Guo Shunhe, also ended its operations. Although the market is desolate, the people are accustomed to diligence and simplicity. Women also work hard and diligently engage in production. There are no cars on the streets, and only a dozen rickshaws. People regard riding in cars as a disgrace. This spirit of perseverance is unmatched by other provinces. I visited Guangxi University and met Principal Ma Jiawei. We were delighted to see each other. I said that Shanghai's industries should pay more attention to inland industries in the future. The establishment of heavy industries should be based inland, which would not only revitalize the rural economy but also avoid danger. Guangxi is a poor province, and there are concerns about the lack of financial resources and talent. In terms of talent, Guangxi University has established four colleges: science, agriculture, engineering, and mining. It is hoped that technical talents will be trained as much as possible to develop the local economy. Young people are fond of studying literature and law. I want to correct this problem. Therefore, Guangxi University does not have colleges of literature and law to achieve industrial salvation of the country. My colleagues and I were very interested in observing the practical spirit of the students of the agriculture and engineering colleges. Principal Ma said that students should not only be students but also soldiers and laborers. So I call the students production soldiers, and we laughed together. Principal Ma inquired about the current situation of vocational education, saying that Guangxi is strongly promoting vocational education, but the issue of employment needs to be studied. I visited the military training of the girls' high school, combining military affairs with learning. This is the case throughout the province, which is admirable. I visited the sulfuric acid plant, tung oil plant, match factory, pharmaceutical factory, etc. The scale is complete. According to Chen Xiongjun, manager of the Export Trade Office, 210,000 tons of tung oil are sold annually, worth more than 10 million silver dollars. Minerals such as tungsten, tin, manganese, and antimony are also increasing. I deeply hope that the industrial and commercial circles of Shanghai and Guangxi can work together to transport and exchange goods between the two sides. In the future, Wuzhou may have hope for commercial recovery.

Ministry of Education: Today's Education Broadcast Program 192

Topic: Lecture on Chemistry

Lecturer: Chen Kezhong

Receiving Institutions: Secondary Schools

Secondary School and Normal School Education Research Conference: This Year's Research on Teaching Methods for Various Subjects 193

Special Solicitation of Teaching Research Reports for Various Subjects from Schools and Solicitation of Learning Experience Reports for Various Subjects from Students; Two Solicitation Methods Have Been Formulated and Announced by the Education Bureau

The Shanghai Education Bureau yesterday instructed the city's municipal and private registered middle schools and normal schools: It is found that the Shanghai Middle School and Normal School Education Research Conference held its second conference of the 24th year on the 13th of this month. It was decided that the central research issues for this year would be "Teaching Methods for Various Subjects" and "National Crisis Education." The bureau has formulated methods for carrying out each research issue separately. It has now been decided by the bureau that, in addition to the research on national crisis education, which should be discussed collectively after the groups are determined, the research on teaching methods for various subjects should start with the solicitation of teaching research reports from teachers and learning experience reports from students from various schools. The materials obtained will be used as reference for research. Two methods for collecting teaching research reports and learning experience reports for various subjects, and a learning experience report form are formulated and printed with this document. The principals of the schools are requested to strictly abide by them and submit them to the bureau for review on time. In addition, this semester, the conference will be divided into two groups: teaching methods and national crisis education. The school should indicate which group it voluntarily joins and the subject of teaching research it identifies (in accordance with Article 11 of the method for collecting teaching research reports for various subjects) on the attached postcard and send it to the bureau within three days of receiving this document for compilation. This is very important. This order is attached with the collection methods as follows:

Collection of Teaching Research Reports 194

Collection Method: Municipal and private registered middle schools and normal schools in this city must submit teaching research reports for various subjects in accordance with this method. Teaching research reports for various subjects are temporarily limited to junior middle schools and junior normal schools. Teaching research reports for various subjects should be compiled by subject in accordance with the subjects stipulated in the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry. When necessary, they should also be compiled by category in accordance with the types of assignments stipulated in the curriculum standards for each subject. The content of teaching research reports for various subjects should be divided into at least the following four items: A. Research on educational objectives; B. Research on teaching time; C. Research on teaching materials; D. Research on teaching methods. The research on teaching objectives should not only elaborate on the meaning of the objectives stipulated in the curriculum standards, but also express detailed opinions based on personal opinions. The research on teaching time should not only cover teaching time in class, but also the allocation of homework time outside of class, all of which should be compiled by grade. The research on teaching materials should not only be based on the teaching material outline stipulated in the curriculum standards and provide detailed critical discussion on its value, but also pay attention to the research on homework materials, all of which should be compiled by grade. The research on teaching methods should not only explore general principles, but also seek concrete and effective solutions to the difficulties encountered in teaching based on practical experience. When necessary, in addition to compiling by grade, it should also be compiled by item according to the different nature of teaching materials. If schools have research experiences or implementation reports other than the above four contents, they should also be compiled together. In principle, each school should submit research reports for at least one subject, which should be determined by the school itself first, but the Education Bureau may change or designate it separately when necessary. After the promulgation of this method, the principal of each school should immediately convene a meeting of teachers and staff or directly determine the subject to be responsible for research and report it to the Education Bureau for filing. After the subject of research is determined, the principal of each school should convene a meeting of teachers responsible for the subject to discuss and draft a report method, which should be jointly drafted by the teachers responsible for the subject. After the teachers responsible for each subject have prepared the research report, it should be submitted to the principal for review and consolidation, or submitted to the faculty and staff meeting for joint discussion, and then the official report should be prepared and submitted to the Education Bureau by April 15th of the 25th year for forwarding to the conference. The quality of the content of the research reports of each school may be listed by the Education Bureau as one of the important evaluations of the schools and teachers in this semester. If there are any shortcomings in this method, the chairman of this conference may revise it at any time. This method shall be formulated by the chairman of this conference and promulgated and implemented by the Education Bureau.

Solicitation of Learning Experience Reports 195

Solicitation Method: This conference, in order to study teaching methods for various subjects and improve teaching effectiveness, specially solicits learning experience reports for various subjects from students of municipal and private registered middle schools and normal schools in the city, and makes a form for distribution to schools to order students to fill in and report. All students of municipal and private registered middle schools and normal schools in this city must fill in the form in accordance with this method. Learning experience reports for various subjects are temporarily limited to junior middle schools and junior normal schools. Learning experience reports for various subjects should be compiled by subject in accordance with the subjects studied. When necessary, they should also be compiled by item according to the types of assignments for each subject. The content of learning experience reports for various subjects is divided into the following items: A. Learning objectives: Why do I want to study this subject? B. Learning interest: How interested am I in this subject? C. Learning time: How do I allocate my homework time outside of regular class time for this subject? D. Learning materials: What are my opinions on the materials I have learned for this subject? In addition to the materials assigned by the teacher, what other supplementary materials do I find myself? E. Learning methods: Do I have a predetermined plan and a certain principle for the learning method of this subject? How does the teacher guide me to learn? In addition to the learning methods guided by the teacher, what other effective methods have I researched myself? F. Difficulties encountered: What difficulties do I encounter in learning this subject? Is there a solution? G. Personal hopes: What hopes do I have for this subject in order to increase learning effectiveness? Whether for the school, for the teacher, for the students, or for myself. H. Other: Do I have any other opinions and experiences on this subject? There is no requirement for the subject to be solicited. Each person can choose one or several subjects, or only one or several items in the assignment category of a certain subject. There is no requirement for the writing style of the solicitation, but the principle is to be detailed and concise. The principal of each school should, after the promulgation of this method, immediately convene the class teachers or responsible counselors of each grade to explain the method, and the class teachers or responsible counselors should guide the students to respond to the solicitation. Under the principle of not hindering the free expression of students, the teachers responsible for each subject may give appropriate guidance before the students respond to the solicitation, but the principle is to provide joint guidance to the entire grade and not to provide direct suggestions. The solicitation reports should be submitted by the students to the class teacher or responsible counselor, and then submitted to the principal for consolidation. After the principal has sorted them by subject and grade, they should be submitted to the Education Bureau for forwarding to the conference. The deadline for each school to submit solicitation reports is April 15th of the 25th year. After the solicitation reports of each school are reviewed by the conference, the Education Bureau will select the best ones for awards. The form for learning each report shall be formulated by this conference and reprinted by each school according to the form. If there are any shortcomings in this method, the chairman of this conference may revise it at any time. This method shall be formulated by the chairman of this conference and promulgated and implemented by the Education Bureau.

Children's Educational Novel: Little Men (2)(0)(9) 196

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

At that moment, Laurie had already slipped into the hall and said a word to the children, and immediately the whole group rushed in, holding hands, forming a circle, dancing around Uncle Plover and Aunt Plover, singing briskly?

"Spring ploughing and summer weeding,

Planting hundreds of grains,

Harvesting abundant crops,

Autumn harvest connects the houses.

The community wine has been drunk,

The happy meeting is coming to an end,

To express gratitude,

There is still one thing,

Planting grains is plentiful,

Planting people is especially urgent,

Lively children,

Cultivating into outstanding talents.

We this evening,

Singing and dancing,

Thank you teachers,

Kindness is like parents."

When singing to the last sentence, the circle gradually converged, until the good professor and his wife were surrounded by many arms, and almost half-hidden by a living wreath formed by many smiling faces—this shows that a kind of "love" has taken root and flourished in every small circle. Because "love" is a flower that grows without choosing soil, accomplishing its wonderful miracle, unchanging through autumn frost and winter snow, blooming with beautiful and fragrant flowers in all seasons, and blessing its recipients and givers. Shanghai Boy Scout Spring Break Trip to Hangzhou: Must Comply with the Council's Circular 197

The Shanghai Boy Scout Council, in view of the fact that many Boy Scouts in the city will travel to Hangzhou during the spring break, in order to unify actions and maintain reputation, specially issued a circular to various groups yesterday, and attached the Hangzhou Travel Management Measures for compliance. The details are explored as follows:

Circular to Various Groups: For information, it is found that the Zhejiang Provincial Boy Scouts are scheduled to hold a conference in Hangzhou on April 4th. It is the spring break, and it is appropriate for each group to take this opportunity to travel to Hangzhou, first to visit the conference to increase the knowledge of the members, and also to visit scenic spots and historical sites to practice outdoor life. In order to reduce the cost of each group's trip to Hangzhou and unify actions in Hangzhou, in addition to negotiating with the Ministry of Railways, all Boy Scouts in the city going to Hangzhou are allowed to reduce the round-trip ordinary ticket price by 50% by referring to the student group travel fare reduction method. Among them, Boy Scouts under the age of 20 are also allowed to calculate the number of people as two people for one person when calculating the number of people, but they are not allowed to take special express trains. A kind of Shanghai Boy Scout Spring Break Hangzhou Travel Management Measures is specially formulated and issued with this document. If the group holds a Hangzhou trip during the spring break, it must comply with it in order to unify actions, strengthen the observation, and protect the reputation of the Boy Scouts in this city.

Travel Management Measures: All groups in this city traveling to Hangzhou during the spring break must comply with this method. After each group has determined the number of people going to Hangzhou and the date and time of departure and return to Shanghai, they can present a petition to send someone to the council to collect a certificate and go to the railway bureau to handle the procedures for earning tickets and booking cars. The date and time of departure and return to Shanghai and the accommodation and meals in Hangzhou are all at the discretion of each group. Boy Scouts from each group in Hangzhou must arrive at the lakeside public stadium before 7:00 am on April 4th to report. The council will send someone to lead the team to visit the Zhejiang Provincial Fifth Congress Review Ceremony, but the following items must be noted: 1. The clothing must comply with the regulations and strive to be clean; 2. The spirit must be invigorated; 3. The military sticks and flags must not be brought; 4. Except for those designated by the council, the other groups must not bring the band. In addition to visiting the Congress Review Ceremony, other sightseeing activities are free, but the following items must be noted: 1. Strictly abide by discipline and must not have excessive behavior; 2. Constantly straighten the clothing and pay attention to the body section; 3. Must not have disrespectful behavior towards friendly groups in this city and Zhejiang Province Boy Scouts. If anyone violates the above points, the council may, based on the report or report, investigate and determine the facts, and give the person in charge of each group and the offending members appropriate punishment, and may order them to return to Shanghai if necessary. Those who strictly abide by discipline and perform well will be commended by the council. The address of the council members in Hangzhou can be inquired at the Lakeside Public Education Center.

Shanghai Blind Children School Fundraising Campaign: April 4th, Chinese and Foreign Boy Scouts Will Donate Along the Way for One Day 198

The School for Blind Children at 290 Hongqiao Road in this city was specially established by British scholar Dr. Chuan Lanya to educate Chinese blind children and enable them to study and learn skills to become useful talents. It has been established for more than 20 years, and the achievements are outstanding. The talents it has cultivated serve in the community and are all competent and happy. It is praised by Chinese and foreign people, and often helps with donations. The large ones, such as the Rotary Club of Shanghai, have donated three craft department houses. Mr. Lister's will donated a fund of 50,000 taels. Minister Song's mother donated 9,000 yuan to promote it. Initially, the school was located in the school building built by Chuan Bo ten donations on Yidingpan Road. However, because the number of applicants is increasing day by day, the original school site is not enough. Four years ago, the original site on Yidingpan Road was sold and more than 20 acres of land were purchased on Hongqiao Road to build 12 houses to expand. As a result, the interest on the fund is difficult to cover the distribution of the business. In addition, the atmosphere of economic downturn covers the whole society, and the sources of various donations are becoming more and more detailed, and it is difficult to continue. Although it has been assisted by Chinese and foreign people over the years, such as Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Minister Song Ziwen, Minister Kong Xiangxi, Wang Zhengting, Li Ming, Liu Hongsheng, and Zhu Shaoping have generously donated huge amounts of money. However, due to the daily development of the business and the addition of a deaf and mute department, it is more costly to teach deaf and mute students to speak, read, and learn art. The school is now scheduled to invite Chinese and foreign Boy Scouts and Chinese and Western gentlemen and ladies on April 4th to hold a one-day donation campaign along the way. However, the school has traditionally received donations from Westerners. I think there are many enthusiastic philanthropists in our country. For this kind of Westerners' enthusiastic education of Chinese disabled children, they will not bear to let it be abandoned halfway. If you are generously donating, you can send it to Chuan Bulao, the principal of the school.

West Youth Eighth Volleyball Championship, Sea Youth Retains Title 203

Yesterday's Russian Team Performance Was Brilliant, But a 2-1 Victory Was Inconsequential

Sea Youth Only Won the First Game, but Retaining the Championship is Still Pleasing

The final match of the Group A of the West Youth Eighth Volleyball League took place last night between Sea Youth and the Russian team, starting at 7:15 PM. In the first round, Sea Youth defeated the Russian team in straight sets, so it was widely expected that Sea Youth would win yesterday's match. However, unexpectedly, the Russian team's performance was full of brilliance, especially Polokoff's serves, which were as fast as cannonballs, leaving Sea Youth helpless. Zheng Yiquan and Mai Bingyao of Sea Youth were still abnormally nervous, but repeatedly made surprising moves, earning the audience's praise. In the end, the Russian team won 2-1, but because of their previous defeat in three games, the championship still belonged to Sea Youth. Spring and Autumn

Snippets 228

— (Yan Maode)

You must know that in an instant, the present will become the past, and the future will become the present. But the age that people live is finite, while time is limitless: within our short period of existence, we must firmly grasp reality and get to work! Don't just wait for tomorrow every day!

Desire has no northern boundary, and life values moderation; it is certainly reasonable to seek the satisfaction of appropriate desires within the realm of possibility. However, engaging in impossible excessive demands will make one a slave to desire for life; a lively mind will be forever trapped in a deep abyss of dissatisfaction, with no time to escape.

What is failure? Philippe said: "Nothing else, failure is just a stepping stone to a higher step." Many successful people are blessed by repeated failures. Without failure, I am afraid that great victories will not be obtained. And for strong people, failure is enough to increase their determination, courage, and make them successful.

Early Spring in the French Park 229

— Zhu Ying

The branches of the withered poplar are forcefully releasing tender green new buds. Although pine needles, cypress leaves, and wintergreen are said to be cold-resistant, when a slightly damp spring breeze blows past, they seem to be breathing softly, turning all the leaves into a charming green color. The small grasses by the pond have also discarded their gray-yellow covers, and their small tender heads have burrowed out of the ground, nodding towards the tender buds of the willow branches, as if saying, "Ha, you're here too?" The water lying quietly in the pond is also wrinkled into fine water patterns on its surface, as if showing a contented and knowing smile.

This is early spring in the French Park, early spring that has just escaped from the harsh winter. The birds on the branches are singing songs at the treetops, chirping and chirping. What are they singing? Hmm, maybe spring love songs. That's right, they are spring love songs. Pairs of young men and women, arm in arm, stepping with rhythmic steps, emerge from this grove, saying (sweet words of spring, full of natural laughter, slowly turning into another grove. It is said that the solitary do not see the change of seasons, what they can feel is only the boredom that grows out of being surrounded by the atmosphere of spring. The little birds on the branches are startled and fly away, their chirping songs stop, and the young men and women arm in arm are also startled and stop walking. A solitary person occasionally lets out a long howl—a cry of boredom.

Western children have all changed into brightly colored clothes, playing lively on the green grass, embellishing the business of early spring. "Moms" are pushing baby carriages, strolling on the grass, their steps so slow, their eyes looking around, looking around at the spring scenery, looking at the special pleasant complexion of the tourists in the spring breeze, watching to their heart's content, and occasionally a smile hangs unconsciously on their lips. The business of spring is exploding in every cell—the damp spring breeze is seductively blowing, blowing every cell to explode.

The sunlight is still so weak, but the park is already so full of business, although the various flowers still do not have any news of budding. Early spring in the French Park is truly like a young and beautiful waitress in a Parisian cafe. The waitress is to be appreciated under electric lights, and the French Park, shrouded in the pale yellow sunlight of early spring, seems even more vivid and pure, and worth cherishing.

The Strange Stone Carver 230

— Zui Qiao

Occasionally chatting with friends, and speaking of the strange stone carver, I couldn't help but listen to it as a myth: He is a bachelor in his fifties, a Ningbo native, who has been in Shanghai for many years. All his actions are the same as ordinary people, except that when eating, he must frequently shake his head to both sides. At the same time, he raises the little fingers of both hands, rising and falling, carefully watching with his eyes on both sides. What is especially strange is that when eating, such as eating fish without spitting out the bones, and eating peanuts and melon seeds without spitting out the shells, he also enjoys it and does not feel the pain of bones pricking his throat at all.

Around 231

— Hong

One year, his wife died of illness. After he took care of the funeral, he did not feel sad, and seemed very satisfied. Moreover, he bought many gifts and ran to his mother-in-law's house, whom he rarely visited. Of course, this made her very surprised. She thought: This stubborn and unapproachable son-in-law has unexpectedly come to the door today, which is something worth studying. So he explained, "The reason why I didn't come before is because you couldn't be considered my mother-in-law, because your daughter was still alive, and might be seduced by bad people, turning her back on me, then you would be someone else's mother-in-law! Now that your daughter is dead, she will naturally return to innocence from now on, so I am here today to formally recognize my mother-in-law." These words of his seem as circuitous and foolish, but he has a deep observation of the present era!

Now, he has been hit by the high tide of unemployment, making him a wanderer. He often lingers at the homes of some of his friends, and his friends also welcome him. At the same time, he also has an unique skill, that is, he can predict sunny and rainy weather without any mistakes. It is said that he now lives in Hongkou. If I have the opportunity, I will definitely ask my friends to accompany me to visit him for a meeting, so that I can see this strange stone hill.

Black Market in Nanjing 232

— Shou Qiu

In Nanjing, if you mention the black market, probably no one doesn't know about it. In fact, the black market in Nanjing has a very long history!

The location of the black market used to be in the area of Erdao Gaojing on Fengfu Road. What about now? It has been changed to Gong Houshan in Chaotian Palace on Jianye Road. Their business hours were originally at night, and they closed the market after the sun came out. Later, in order to prevent improper trading at night, the Capital Police Department specially ordered them to change to a "flea market," from dawn until nine or ten o'clock. So the black market in Nanjing is already a misnomer.

The main people in the Nanjing black market can probably be said to be the garbage collectors, because there are so many garbage collectors in Nanjing. During the day, they carry garbage baskets to homes to buy old and used things, and after returning, they use some procedures to sort them out, and then bring them to the black market to sell. With this transfer, they can get a lot of profit!

The bargaining in the black market has a kind of code language. If you understand this code language, you can buy cheap things. Otherwise, not only will you not get a bargain, but you may even be fooled!

According to a garbage collector, there are probably thousands of people who rely on this black market to live, because if there is no black market, they will have nowhere to sell the things they buy! This is indeed the truth.

If you have nothing to do, you can often go there for a walk, perhaps you can encounter some strange things. My friend Mr. Wang once bought an ancient inkstone for the price of a string of money, but this is a matter of luck.

Xiaoxitian 233

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 24: Valuing Beauty and Dismissing the Porter, Parting with Love; Ambitious and Strong-Footed, a Robust Man Flees to the Wilderness

Zhiqian pondered for a while, then suddenly jumped up and said: I don't have anything particularly important to do, but I have many friends, and I should say goodbye to them. In fact, I'm really leaving in a hurry, but my friends can forgive me. I'll write a farewell notice and publish it in the newspaper for a few days. Yourong said: That's right, a great man does things, he must be able to lift up and let go. Now that Mr. Cheng has decided to make this long journey, these small social programs can be put aside. Now Mr. Guo and Mr. Cheng are chatting with me here. Mr. Cheng can return to his room to take care of his private affairs. If you have anything to discuss before the trip, you can talk about it tonight. If there are any unfinished matters, you can handle them early tomorrow morning, and there will still be time. As he spoke, he held his chest high and his face was tight. That appearance, however, taught the people following him that they had to cheer up. Zhiqian stood up, rubbed his hands together repeatedly, and smiled: I am not worthy of the three words "great man," but I should accept County Chief Zhou's teaching of "lift up and let go." As he spoke, he happily jumped away. Eighteen hours later, it was noon the next day. At the entrance of Xiaoxitian, a long-distance bus was parked. The car was covered with a yellow canvas soft top, and a small rectangular flag was inserted on the top, which read "Western Travel Group." Inside Xiaoxitian, several people in short clothes were carrying boxes and nets to the car. Behind the luggage, a large group of people came out. Zhiqian changed into traveling clothes, covered himself with a woolen coat, held a cane in his hand, carried a camera box in one hand, his face full of smiles, and walked out among the crowd. Li Shilian, Zhang Jie, and the Director Chang of the Education Department were all closely following behind to see him off. Li Shilian walked along the way, whispering to Zhiqian: If you can't find a way in Xi'an, you'll be embarrassed to return to Jiangnan. (419)

Local Customs and Anecdotes

Anecdotes of Yuncheng 234

— Mingdao

Yuncheng, Shanxi, is a remote and secluded place, and few are familiar with its name. The local customs are simple and honest, the land is fertile, and most of the residents are engaged in agriculture. They are simple and do not interfere in external affairs. It is truly like the so-called "ideal world" described by Lao Tzu, where neighboring countries can see each other, and the sounds of chickens and dogs can be heard, but people do not interact with each other until they die. It is no less than a paradise. A friend from there described the local customs and folkways, and there are many amusing things, so I have recorded them haphazardly as follows:

Transportation in Yuncheng is inconvenient. Although there is a highway to Taiyuan in the north and Tongguan in the south, the road is rugged and uneven, and cars must circle up and down the mountains. If the driver is slightly careless, it is easy to cause the disaster of being crushed to pieces. Therefore, the general public regards it as a daunting task and would rather sit in a heavy mule cart. The streets there are not very clean, and most of them are dirt roads. When it rains, the roads are full of mud, and when the weather is clear, the ash and sand hit people. Therefore, every household hangs a broom on the door, and every time they return from the street, they must take a broom and sweep their body and feet before entering the house.

There are many troops stationed around, but they are very friendly to the people and there is absolutely no harassment. There are few theft cases throughout the year, and there is almost a wind of not closing the doors at night. This is because every household is frugal and there are no extremely poor people, and very few outsiders come to the common land. In the market, everyone used to use silver dollars, and there were no paper bills. Now that the currency system has been changed, the sound of clinking silver coins will almost disappear. I wonder what the situation will be for the general hoarders?

Although education in Yuncheng is not very developed, there is also a middle school, as well as a female normal school, and there are also several elementary schools, but the level of the students is very naive, and the time for reading is from 7:00 in the morning to 9:00 at night. Except for two meals in the morning and evening, they are all reading. Most of the students read by rote, murmuring like an old woman chanting scriptures, which is very laughable.

The custom of valuing men over women has not yet been reformed, so women rarely interact with foreign guests on weekdays, and there are very few traces on the streets. New brides are hidden in their boudoirs all year round and cannot see outsiders for three years, otherwise they will be condemned as rude. However, women have a great opportunity for liberation around the Lantern Festival in the first month of the lunar calendar. During the three days of the tenth, fifteenth and sixteenth, the area must hang lanterns to celebrate the good night. The so-called fire tree and silver flower, the grand occasion of Jinwu's ban, can still be seen in Yuncheng. Women from all over the city flock out, crowding the streets to watch the lanterns, taking it as a pleasure. Even if they do not return late at night, they are also free to do so, but in a year, there are only these three days of leisure. The陋custom of showing off small feet is also a despicable and strange thing.

What is showing off small feet? The women of Yuncheng all bind their feet, just like the women of the nineteenth century. The happiness of natural feet is not available, and instead, they take pride in golden lotuses that stick to the ground, three inches narrow. Every year during the Lantern Festival, they often sit at the door during the day, stretching out their pairs of small feet, exposing them to the sunlight, which is called showing off small feet. Embroidered shoes with intricate designs, are a kind of psychology of jealousy and competition for beauty, which is laughable and pitiful. Frivolous men wander the streets, discussing and commenting on their feet for fun. Is it thin? Is it pointed? A word of praise is more glorious than luxurious clothes. If the lotus petals of a certain family's women are praised, their family will regard it as a great honor.

Around the Lantern Festival, there are many swing sets in the streets. People of all ages, men and women, must place themselves on the swing and swing once, thinking that they can avoid a year's disasters. However, the swing set is very high, and those who are good at it swing back and forth, flying in the air, and onlookers often clap their hands and praise. Once, an old woman lost her grip and fell from the swing set and died. Isn't this the harm of superstition?

There are very few folk entertainments. During the New Year, I suddenly heard that there was a movie screening in the Guandi Temple. My friend thought that this was a great opportunity not to be missed, so he hired a car with several friends and drove to the place to see the grand occasion on the screen, because it was very far away. Unexpectedly, the so-called movie was just a huge white screen on the stage. Lights were set up behind the screen, and several people held paper-cut figures, moving back and forth, making a fighting posture. Watching it was really laughable. The local men and women sat and watched, savoring it with relish. My friend couldn't help but call it a grievance and returned in annoyance. Only later did I realize that this kind of movie was originally used to please the gods. Therefore, it is called shadow play and cannot be called film, and from this "end" we can also know the local culture.

Notes on What I Saw 235

— (Shijiu)

A certain county in eastern Zhejiang has always had a strong feudal color. A few days ago, having nothing to do, I strolled around and suddenly saw a "strange announcement" in a small shop, which was posted high on the wall, making people unable to help but laugh. It is recorded as follows:

Good News　Capital News

Mr. X Yin X of your esteemed residence　Sincerely

The National Government of Nanjing orders that a certificate be issued　Having

Appointed Chairman of the XX Province Government　This Order

The characters were written in red ink. "Chairman" was mistakenly written as "Master of the Mat," which is very laughable! As for the honorable name of that gentleman, it is currently not among the provincial chairmen.

The announcement is yellow, and the characters are handwritten and do not exist. It is hereby declared together. Horizontally. At the top, the party and national flags are drawn crossing each other, and the shape is quite clumsy. In the second line, "simply made his name and a certain provincial seal," the character after "Yin" and the third line "He" names are all left blank. He was honored to be "Master of the Mat," so the meaning is quite literal.
