Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Special Issue

The Nursing Profession in China Today (Part 2) 236

Li Lingdong

(III) Lack of Teaching Materials and Qualified Teachers: Teaching materials are the primary tool for achieving nursing education, and suitable teaching materials can affect the fate and future of the entire nursing profession. However, China has always lacked suitable teaching materials. Even if textbooks exist, they are either translated from foreign countries, failing to adapt to the needs of China's social position, or they are outdated and full of shortcomings. Since we believe that teaching materials should be valued, we cannot ignore the issue of qualified teachers who manage these materials. Because to popularize or reform nursing education, it is necessary to rely on teachers' teaching skills to achieve practical results. However, most teachers in nursing schools are currently physicians or nurses who teach part-time. They have not received adequate teacher training and lack practical teaching skills. In addition, the heavy medical workload in the hospital and the busy work schedule prevent them from coming to class on time. The knowledge imparted to nursing students and their nursing skills are reduced invisibly. Therefore, the lack of teaching materials and qualified teachers is indeed an obstacle to the advancement of the nursing profession.

B. Analysis of Types of Nursing Talents

Nurses Who Sell Dog Meat Under the Guise of Sheep's Head: This is a common problem among male nurses in China. What does it mean to "sell dog meat under the guise of sheep's head"? It refers to male nurses who have received considerable training in the nursing profession, possess specialized nursing skills, but fail to strive to develop their careers and utilize their skills to serve society. Instead, they abandon their profession, put up a doctor's signboard, and deceive the public. We attribute this to the lack of social organization, which prevents them from achieving a stable life. For the sake of making a living and satisfying their hunger, they resort to taking risks and engaging in abnormal professions. It is hoped that the nursing school authorities will pay attention to this issue.

Nurses Who Seek Marriage Partners: In everyone's mind, the nursing profession is generally recognized as a specialized profession for women. Facts tell us that it is very simple: women have gentle temperaments and delicate minds, which make them more than capable of the job. Since the nursing profession is dominated by women with unique skills, why are there so few older female nurses serving society and benefiting society during the past fifty years? This raises a question that makes people wonder. The reason is that they fundamentally fail to understand the true meaning of life and the true meaning of occupational service. They do not consider their profession as a lifelong career to serve humanity forever. Once they find an ideal husband, they gradually retreat from their service vocation due to the leisure and comfort of family life and leave their profession. This cycle continues endlessly. This problem of the scarcity of elderly female nurses in China has clearly given us the correct answer. Therefore, these are nurses who seek marriage partners. However, it is hoped that female nurse comrades will think calmly and encourage the future.

Nurses Who Embrace Pessimism: What are nurses who embrace pessimism? They not only do not believe that China's nursing future has hope and brightness, but also believe that the entire Chinese nursing community is already doomed. They think that even if they struggle, they cannot make society recognize the importance of the nursing profession. It is better to seek a full stomach quietly, which they feel is more leisurely and comfortable. Of course, we have no possibility of refuting this, because the reality of Chinese society is before us. However, what we can answer is that China's nursing future is extremely hopeful, as long as the entire nursing community stands on a single front and works hard. If everyone contributes a bit of strength to push forward, perhaps one day the Chinese public will recognize the greatness of our nursing profession.

Nurses With a Sense of Failure: Although they are not absolutely pessimistic and can still acknowledge the existence of victory in the nursing future, they lack deep self-confidence. This is because they once cried out and struggled loudly for the nursing profession to achieve victory in the future, but society disappointed and discouraged them. They believe that if Chinese society cannot be improved one day, the nursing profession will never have a way out. We can say that they should continue their efforts, arouse fervent emotions, courageous spirit, and resolute will to conquer the social environment and launch the great nursing profession of China.

In summary, the general observation of the nursing profession and the analysis of talents clearly show us that although the Chinese nursing community has more than fifty years of history, it has not yet escaped the path of darkness. How should we start reforming the nursing profession in the future, and what is our central goal of effort? Some say that nursing education is the vanguard of reform, and we cannot deny it. However, the independence of nursing administration is the means to achieve nursing education and a necessary process to develop the basic organization of the nursing profession. From this point of view, nursing administration is the prerequisite to solving the problems of the nursing profession and the central goal of future efforts. We sincerely hope that all Chinese nurse comrades will strive together with a common will and cooperative spirit to make nursing administration independent, complete its sovereignty, and launch the glorious path of Chinese nursing.

Diphtheria Prevention 237

— Yao Xingshu

Diphtheria is one of the most brutal diseases and the most critical of acute infectious diseases. In recent years, with the increasing convenience of transportation, the epidemic of diphtheria has become more rampant. Even in advanced countries with relatively perfect sanitary facilities, the morbidity rate of diphtheria has been gradually increasing in recent times; patients with malignant diphtheria have also increased compared to the past. Statistics from experts all prove this to be true. Our country is located in both temperate and tropical zones, and our sanitation efforts are very rudimentary. Although accurate statistical reports on the number of patients, deaths, and economic losses have not been obtained, it is easy to imagine the extent of the problem. Alas! What we hear and see tells us that our people suffer greatly from this disease.

Since the German scientist Behring discovered diphtheria antitoxin therapy in 1890, according to European and American statistics, the mortality rate has decreased by one-third compared to the past. However, reports from Japanese scholars show that the mortality rate still exceeds 20%. This indicates that the therapeutic effect has not reached our ideal state. This is because the timing of treatment varies, and the physical strength of patients differs. However, in recent years, the incidence of this disease has been decreasing year by year in the United States, which is the result of efforts in prevention. Therefore, advocating prevention as a comprehensive strategy is the primary task of those who seek public health.

There are various methods of preventing this disease. The so-called general prevention methods require healthy people to be absolutely isolated from patients with the disease. Various excreta from patients should not be placed arbitrarily but should be received in containers pre-filled with disinfectants. In addition, utensils and clothing that have come into contact with the patient may have germs attached and serve as a medium for transmission, so they must be thoroughly disinfected. In short, once a patient with this disease is discovered, it is best to send them to an infectious disease isolation hospital. If not, one should choose a room to live in to avoid close contact with many people. However, it is easy to say all this, but difficult to do. First, there are few infectious disease isolation hospitals in our country; second, the public lacks medical and health knowledge. As for subcutaneous injection of diphtheria antitoxin, the so-called passive immunization method, has been adopted for a long time. Although it can provide temporary immunity to diphtheria (i.e., not being infected), its effect lasts only three weeks. After that, there is still a risk of infection. Moreover, after once undergoing this method, there is a risk of causing allergic reactions when injecting antitoxin again. Therefore, its application is limited to times when prevention is urgently needed, such as prevention for those who care for patients, doctors, siblings, parents, family members, etc., or when there is an outbreak in schools, boarding schools, and other group living situations. In terms of its efficacy, it cannot be said to be without its flaws.

Today's people, if they have a slight degree of

(Continued on page 16)

A World View of Tuberculosis Statistics (2) 238

— Ding Huikang

Then, what is the value of the decrease in tuberculosis mortality rates in various countries? This kind of problem cannot be strictly generalized, because tuberculosis cannot be compared identically in various countries, regions, different ethnic groups, and different ages.

The transmission of tuberculosis has different timeliness and aggressiveness in different regions. Due to cultural differences, the transmission may be faster or slower, earlier or later in a certain ethnic group.

Observing the world from the perspective of tuberculosis invasion, according to Biraud, attention should first be paid to European countries, the United States of North America, Canada, Australia, New Zealand, and Japanese cities, because in the above-mentioned regions, it is convenient to diagnose and detect the causes of tuberculosis at an early stage. In addition, cases of tuberculosis mortality that do not change or even increase include countries in Central and South America, the Indian archipelago, France, and China. Tuberculosis that has spread from Europe to Africa has mostly spread to central Africa, while tuberculosis in French North Africa and South Africa has once invaded but has now receded.

In the most recent century, (Rossele) Norway has maintained the lowest number of tuberculosis deaths. In 1910, Denmark had the lowest number. In 1920, the death rate in the Netherlands was even lower than in Norway. After the war, statistics from Switzerland, the United Kingdom, Sweden, and Germany showed that the death rate decreased. Recent observations show that Germany has the lowest tuberculosis death rate compared to other countries, making it the country with the fewest tuberculosis deaths in Europe and worldwide. According to the research of Greenwood and Wolff in the United Kingdom, tuberculosis death rates are inherently low in industrialized countries, but within industrialized countries, the death rates are higher in industrial areas than in other areas.

In his book on the reduction of tuberculosis, Dann believes that medical improvements and Lobert Koch's discoveries are equally important, making the contagiousness of tuberculosis fully understood and preventable worldwide.

Tuberculosis statistics in Canada are very high, possibly due to a broader understanding of the disease, especially among indigenous people. The death rate in Canada is seven and a half times higher than that of other ethnic groups, with the highest mortality occurring between the ages of ten and fourteen.

In British Australia, the age of tuberculosis infection is relatively late. Hone found in a hospital that only 18.2% of children around the age of thirteen had a positive Pirquet reaction.

The situation of tuberculosis in India is relatively bad, and the death rate is very high, with 31 cases of tuberculosis death per 10,000 people each year. The transmission process is mostly due to severe patients in cities being sent to the countryside for treatment, thereby spreading the infection widely. Public health and general conditions are very poor. Treatment centers and sanatoriums are very lacking. Furthermore, due to the lack of a national anti-tuberculosis organization, anti-tuberculosis work cannot be successful. Moreover, the bad weather makes it easier for tuberculosis bacteria to grow. Due to the lack of immunity to tuberculosis infection, the course of tuberculosis is mostly acute and severe, and mostly belongs to mixed infections, with a very large number of patients. However, the course of glandular tuberculosis, bone and joint tuberculosis, and joint tuberculosis is safer in India.

In Italy, the density of households in cities, the lack of large squares and gardens, and the fact that workshops are mostly too small are all major causes of tuberculosis spread, making it the most common disease among the people. In countries such as the Scandinavian countries and the Netherlands, the annual number of deaths is less than the number of hospital beds nationwide. In countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany, the number of deaths and the number of hospital beds are almost the same. In France, there are two deaths for every hospital bed. In Italy, there are five deaths for every hospital bed. In Sardinia, not only is the public health situation very bad, but there are also many malaria cases, bad streets, and dust flying, making treatment difficult. Therefore, the tuberculosis death rate in Italy began to decrease in 1925 and continued until 1930. Statistics on pulmonary tuberculosis have decreased by 32%, and other tuberculosis has decreased by 15%. The anti-tuberculosis work was implemented by the fascist government, and in 1927, compulsory tuberculosis insurance was implemented, with excellent results. The mortality rate for Italian women between the ages of five and nineteen is very high.

Page 16

Even those with a primary school education know that vaccination can prevent the occurrence of smallpox. The safety of vaccination and its effectiveness in preventing smallpox infection can be said to be well-known. The diphtheria automatic immunization method that I want to describe is also similar. Unfortunately, there is a lack of promoters, and the people lack understanding. What has become a past event in Europe and the United States is regarded as a novel discovery in our country. This is not only true for medical and health knowledge. Alas! I really don't know in what year and month the knowledge of diphtheria automatic immunization methods will be as widely spread in the minds of the public as vaccination is for preventing smallpox today.

The diphtheria automatic immunization method has been achieved after many European and American scholars have exhausted their efforts. The drug used is called anatoxin. The manufacturing method does not need to be described in this article. However, in the future, there is no need to worry about allergic reactions when injecting any antitoxin. The power to prevent the occurrence of diphtheria is also better, and the side effects are mild. It is indeed a landmark progress in diphtheria prevention methods and is worth our promotion.

This drug must be injected subcutaneously when applied and can be performed at any time. Statistically, children between the ages of one and seven suffer from diphtheria the most, so this age group should be vaccinated first. The more ideal approach is to administer this preventive injection to children between the ages of nine and twelve months, preferably in the spring. Because the morbidity rate of children after one year old is very high, and the disease is prevalent in the cold winter months, preventive injections in the spring allow sufficient immunity to develop, thereby avoiding illness during the diphtheria-prone winter. Moreover, according to scholars' research, it takes three to six months for immunity to form after injection, so injection should be done as early as possible.

This preventive method has been proven by scholars to be effective, with a long immunity time. Even after more than four years of injection, its effectiveness is still preserved, and some say that immunity can last a lifetime. However, a small number of those injected may feel pain and mild redness at the injection site, but it will disappear after a few months, with no other side effects occurring. It is not more painful than vaccination, but two injections are required.

The effectiveness of diphtheria antitoxin treatment cannot be denied. However, as the saying goes, "The best doctor treats the disease before it occurs." To medicate after the disease has occurred is the worst strategy. Moreover, the application of antitoxin has side effects that cannot be ignored. You all know the danger of diphtheria and the speed of its transmission, so you must hope to obtain a safe, simple, and effective prevention method to seek personal health and increase family happiness. Therefore, in addition to paying attention to general methods, performing preventive injections with anatoxin is the best way, and I sincerely recommend it.

Common Sense on Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene (82): What is Cataract? 239

— Tang Renjin

Among eye diseases, there is what is called cataract. It is caused by the clouding of the lens. The color of the cloudy part is grayish-white, so it is specifically called cataract. The position of the lens is in the middle of the iris and the vitreous body. Its shape is like a convex mirror. The front is connected to the iris and the anterior chamber. The center of the front is called the anterior pole. The back is connected to the vitreous body. The center of the back is called the posterior pole. The part where the front and back surfaces meet is called the equatorial part. The lens also occupies an important position in the refraction of light and has a regulatory effect. The lens is colorless and transparent in the neonatal period. As it ages, it becomes slightly yellow. As it ages to old age, it becomes more yellow-brown. But how can the lens become cloudy and form a cataract? This is due to various reasons. The reasons are briefly described below.

Congenital Causes: Congenital cataract is caused by developmental disorders of the lens or by secondary eye diseases during fetal life. It can also occur during systemic diseases or nutritional disorders. And there is often a genetic relationship.

Age-Related Causes: Cataracts occur most often in older people around the age of 40 or 50. In ophthalmology, it is called senile cataract. The most common cataract in clinical practice is this type of senile cataract. Its true cause is still unknown. It can only be considered as a senile change.

Causes of Systemic Diseases: During the course of diabetes, the lens can often become cloudy. This is called diabetic cataract.

Causes of Complications: In cases of iritis, cyclitis, vitreous opacities, and glaucoma, the lens often becomes cloudy due to nutritional disorders. This is called complicated cataract.

Traumatic Causes: When foreign objects enter, surgical damage, and penetrating injuries such as cuts, stabs, and gunshot wounds occur, the lens capsule can often rupture, causing aqueous humor to enter the lens through the wound and become cloudy. This is called traumatic cataract.

Diagram of the Lens 240

Ⅰ Lens Ⅱ Anterior pole Ⅲ Posterior pole Ⅳ Equatorial part Ⅴ Pupil Ⅵ Iris Ⅶ Vitreous body

Brief Explanation of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (85) 241

— Hu Jiayan

Section 8 Surgical Treatment

If the artificial surgery of the patient has resulted in an effect, the situation of the changes of the lesion itself, of course, has to be determined with auscultation, percussion, and X-ray procedure. But in the clinical aspects, one can see that the coughing stops, the amount of sputum decreases, the tuberculosis bacillus disappears from the sputum, the temperature drops, the blood sedimentation reaction gradually slows down, the body weight increases, etc.; these are all characteristics of progress! Patients can understand it! The two most obvious characteristics are the temperature normalizing and the weight increasing. The longer such progress takes, the more effective it will be: Therefore, the artificial pneumothorax procedure is not to be limited in one or two times; it should be practiced over a long period. Usually, it's about a period of three months, six months, or a year, and sometimes it can last for three or four years: but if the patient has no good progress mentioned above after the surgery, then it is an exception.

The achievements of artificial pneumothorax for the disease have been described above, but readers should know that artificial pneumothorax is not an easy surgery. If one is not careful, and the needle breaks the pulmonary vein, it will immediately cause air embolism. This is one of the most dangerous complications. The patient will immediately fall into death, and there is no first aid method. In addition, emphysema and exudate are also very common, especially exudate is most likely to occur after surgery, accounting for almost 50%. If the amount of fluid is too large, there is a tendency to develop empyema, and the result is still incurable. Therefore, the implementation of artificial pneumothorax surgery, first, must choose an experienced doctor, and second, must be performed under X-ray fluoroscopy. Because the destination of the needle must be selected where the two leaves of the pleura are not yet healed, otherwise it will be a mistake. This layer can't be fully determined by auscultation and percussion. As for how to perform the surgery, how to install the equipment, how to pay attention to X-ray fluoroscopy, and the amount of air injected each time, etc.; these are all knowledge that experts should have, and the average patient does not need to know so much in detail, so this edition also omitted them all!

Q&A on Common Sense of Teeth (25) 242

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 123) How should a toothbrush be placed after use?

Answer: After brushing your teeth, you should wash the toothbrush clean. It is best to wash it with boiling water, and then forcefully drain the water. Hang it in a clean, dust-free place and let it dry. In summer, to avoid mosquitoes and flies, you can find a way to cover it, but do not put it in a small, airtight box, which hinders the evaporation of water.

(Question 124) Can a new toothbrush be used immediately?

Answer: Most of the toothbrushes sold in the market have not been strictly disinfected. Sometimes the bristles are attached with anthrax bacilli, which may cause annoying infectious diseases. For the sake of caution, you should boil the newly purchased toothbrush in water for a quarter of an hour every day, and then you can use it after boiling it two or three times. At the very least, it must be soaked in boiling water.

(Question 125) What method should be used to remove food debris that cannot be brushed away when brushing your teeth?

Answer: When food debris is embedded in the middle of the teeth, you can use a toothpick to pick it out when the toothbrush can't brush it away. There is also another method, which is to use silk thread to press into the teeth and move it up and down to remove the food debris in the middle.

(Question 126) What points should be paid attention to when using a toothpick?

Answer: Improper use of toothpicks is more harmful than beneficial. The following four points should be paid attention to: Do not use metal or other hard toothpicks to pick your teeth. Toothpicks must be made of wood that is flexible and slightly elastic, and must be disinfected and polished. When using a toothpick, do not injure the gums. Most people are accustomed to using too much force and forcibly inserting it into the teeth until the gums bleed. Do not develop the habit of chewing toothpicks, so as not to injure the soft tissues in the mouth due to the tight pressure of the toothpick or the stimulation of wood chips.

Beyond the large headlines such as "Germany Opposes Demilitarized Zones," "French Finance Minister Raises Military Expenditure, House Passes Short-Term Loan with Unprecedented Majority," "U.S. Navy Conducts Large-Scale Exercises in Preparation for Future Wars," "Soviet Russia Deploys Strong Forces to Aigun," and "Newly Appointed Commander of the Kwantung Army, Ueda, Issues Important Inauguration Statement," we also see a piece of news that is both laughable and lamentable: "Bingzi Disaster Relief Dharma Assembly Initiators Meeting Held Yesterday."

However, it is certain that those two "Mongolian-Tibetan Grand Masters" have "presided" over several "Dharma Assemblies."

Next, we naturally have to talk about the merits accumulated from the past "Dharma Assemblies." Speaking of merits, it would take too long to explain. While people are making a lot of noise with "demilitarized zones," "raising military expenditure," and "naval fleet exercises," what kind of achievements will the Bingzi Disaster Relief Dharma Assembly produce for us to see?

Graveyard 244

— Ye Ge

The people of the village were horrified and dazed because an astonishing and strange event occurred not far from their graveyard one drizzly evening. The victim, the sentry Pan Desheng, reported to the mansion of Liu Tuanzong (Head of the Local Militia) the next morning with a bloody face and a limp.

"This thing, the situation, happened like this, ah, Mr. Tuanzong..." the sentry said uneasily. "It was raining, and there was not a single star in the graveyard. It was gloomy, and a nightjar was hiding on an old pine tree, calling out..."

Liu Tuanzong, having just woken up from a half-asleep state, leaned on a large embroidered cushion and looked at his unfortunate sentry with an impatient frown: why didn't he even wash the blood off his face? Desheng was slightly flustered, constantly wiping his forehead with his dirty sleeve, even though he didn't feel hot or stuffy. So, again...

"...According to the usual practice, Mr. Tuanzong, God is above, I never lie. I, following the habits of a good soldier, shouldered my gun, puffed out my chest, and ran back and forth there, guarding this road that passes through the graveyard and leads to Luoyang. Sometimes it was the nightjar wailing mournfully, sometimes it was the sound of raindrops hitting the treetops with a rustling sound; although it was so frighteningly desolate, I was not even slightly alarmed by it. Really, Mr. Tuanzong, I was not afraid... (He swallowed a mouthful of saliva with difficulty).

"But the rain kept getting heavier, and half of my body was soaked. So, I hid under that old pine tree, squatting down. The nightjar was always wailing so sadly, and the raindrops were always sounding so monotonously; but I was not afraid." Really, Mr. Tuanzong, I was smoking.

"It went on like this for quite some time, maybe twenty minutes, maybe half an hour, I can't remember clearly, in short, it went on for quite some time. Suddenly, a gust of wind blew from the graveyard, whistling loudly in the darkness. Then I saw that strange scene: a ball of fire emitting blue flames in the distance, in that graveyard shrouded in darkness. Mr. Tuanzong, you may not believe it: I was not afraid, just slightly shocked. I lifted my gun. I commanded myself in a low voice: "Ready"! But that ball of fire started moving, moving so fast. Under the light of the flames, I seemed to see a large group of disheveled shadows wriggling. (Mr. Tuanzong was greatly shocked at this time. His well-groomed, fair face slowly turned from flushed to pale.) At this time, (the sentry's dirty lips also began to tremble), Mr. Tuanzong, you may not believe it, I was still not afraid, I gripped my gun even tighter. They were still wriggling there, wriggling, chasing me closer and closer. For the sake of my duty, I shouted loudly at them: "Password"? They did not respond, just stopped for a moment, then howled sharply, as if answering me. So, I got angry and secretly commanded myself: "Fire"! The muzzle of the gun sprayed smoke, but this had no effect on them at all. They were wriggling...

"Finally, they reached in front of me. They were a group of naked people covered in black hair, with gleaming eyes. They surrounded me and attacked me with flames. In such a situation, even if it were a god, I believe, Mr. Tuanzong, would inevitably be slightly frightened. But I waved my bayonet and gun and fought with them. People might ask: why did you fight them? Why didn't you sneak away? Then I would answer: for my duty, sir!

"What happened next was what happened the second morning. I was paralyzed in a pile of graves (this fact was later confirmed to Mr. Tuanzong). The gun was gone... As for how long I fought with those demons last night, and how I was defeated, I can't remember clearly at all now...

Tuanzong was a believer in ghosts. He often said that he heard ghosts crying. He believed that in such a graveyard full of stacked corpses, the haunting of ghosts was inevitable and common. But what did the ghosts want with the gun? So, he yawned, waved his hand, and Desheng stepped out of the mansion.

In the afternoon, Desheng was sitting with a strange man in a secluded corner of a small teahouse about five li away from the village, silently sipping tea. The strange man was holding the cup, lightly sipping it on his lips, then slowly putting it down: "Then you?..."

"Of course, I'll leave immediately. Old friend, you can imagine how uneasy I was after receiving that letter! My parents worked so hard to give me this body, but they ended up suffering from floods and hunger at home. Do you think a son can have peace of mind when he is working outside? Alas!..." Desheng replied in a low voice, tears almost dripping down.

"Will the regimental headquarters investigate?" The stranger asked anxiously, looking at him again.

"Investigate my ass, anyway, Tuanzong believed it. These two days, I will ask my brothers to tell another lie and slip away, damn it."

The stranger nodded, sipped the last of the tea from the cup, stood up, paid the money, and went out with Desheng. In a secluded place on the corner, he quietly handed Desheng three ten-yuan bills and said in a low voice: "It's not that I'm not friendly enough, it's just that it's only worth this much!"

They shook hands and parted ways.

A week after this incident, Desheng was assigned to guard the graveyard again. But the next day, besides a pool of blood and torn strips of gray clothing torn from his body, there was nothing else. This story is still being talked about by people with unease.

New Station 246

— You Qi

"Two more days, today we'll rest at Xin Station, tomorrow night we'll rely on Tongzi." Old Zhang Tou said this to the coolies around the table while eating breakfast, his face sinking, swallowing the rest of his words.

Following the road paved along Songkan, our smoke and dust rose. Although the road is not very magnificent in terms of construction, it undoubtedly provides great assistance to passing travelers and business operators.

"Fifteen streams clear the mountains, new graves in the fields where people weep, may I ask you lady why you weep, oh, my good husband!"

"Turtle, you old bastard!" another person cursed.

Affection is not limited to any class. When desire rushes into the heart, that tingling feeling teases the flames of lust, and one can't help but mutter. As the hot sun shone on our heads, they opened their throats and sang boldly.

"Little Ma Wu, only you know how to cause trouble, sixty li to Xin Station, buck up!" A young coolie said with a laugh.

"Let alone sixty, eighty is nothing in my eyes, but there's one thing, we have to rest at Xionghuang Temple for a while, so we can have a good puff, and I guarantee we'll be as fast as flying when we pick up our feet."

Ma Wu laughed, the coolie laughed, and everyone else laughed. "A few more puffs" deeply penetrated everyone's heart, and there was a common expectation.

Twenty-five li is nothing to walk on the road, so we came into contact with Xionghuang Temple.

On the way, it is not difficult to meet merchants coming and going, but here, it is simply a miracle. When our group's smoke and dust covered Xionghuang Temple, unexpectedly, there was another group of smoke and dust inside, preparing to break out of that gloomy encirclement. They also had dozens of coolies, and several foremen, and the goods seemed to be no less than this batch. Look, those delicate girls, holding coarse grains of rice and simple vegetables, looked dazed. How could they have imagined this scene outside of a happy family?

The coolies were messing around, gone, in twos and threes, all with the same hope.

This time, Old Tie changed his attire, tying the large bamboo hat on his back, wrapping his head tightly with a cloth, and twisting a butterfly knot on his forehead, looking like a complete hero from afar. No, once, twice, the group of people in front followed Old Tie away. As a result, Ma Wu, Mao Tou, and another person whose name I don't know disappeared. The foreman's head was hit with an iron bar, and he was anxious and jumped around, but it was useless.

"These turtles, if I see them, I won't beat them half to death!" the young foreman swore.

Time was pressing, not allowing for a long stay. The person responsible for this was naturally unable to shirk responsibility. The young foreman temporarily grabbed a temporary worker to shoulder the flower basket, and Old Zhang Tou, who was over sixty, put the lighter rattan basket on his head.

Being a foreman is not easy. One must be able to attract people, and be able to subdue people to listen to orders. To become a master in the trade, one must accept all kinds of tempers. Now, although the treatment is better, Old Zhang looked at his beard at this old age. If the coolies escape, he will have to pick up this heavy burden himself! Saying this, he sighed.

After a moment of silence, the young foreman finally broke the deadlock—

"You can't treat them with kindness. They will definitely stay at Xin Station tonight. We'll go there to find out."

The load was on Old Zhang's shoulders, his back was sweating, dripping straight down, his left arm swaying!

"Green grass flowers in front..." Like other coolies, he also chanted the usual jargon on the mountain road.

Travel Companion 247

— Zhi Fu

Starting from Muzha, going out of Shimat, is this boundless desert, at least eighty or so li to Kulun.

There are no mountains or water here, only Kees Fu and his travel companion - the camel - on a stretch of sand.

- The sky is gloomy, and there is no sign of habitation all around. Travelers and livestock are hurrying on their way -

Sarala - a huge wind swept in from the front, and a mass of soil the size of a black pile fell in front of me.

The camel is also old, and it used to be unafraid of these things. This year, it has encountered storms and desert waves, and it is simply a little afraid, and cannot catch up! Its hooves are sinking into the sand, as if they have taken root, and it cannot get up.

"Old beast! You have enough provisions, why can't you catch up? Humph! Getting worse every year......!" Kees Fu was a little angry, cursing fiercely.

But the animal ignored him.

"......"

The sky became even gloomier, and the desert waves rose and fell, connecting and sounding again. Even Kees Fu was a little worried...

"I'm afraid that animal will fall!"

He looked at the sky, sighed, and a stream of hot air rushed from his lips, passing through the top of his head, and gradually condensing into water droplets on that leather earmuff, as if about to drip down.

Cold, not the first day it's been cold today, hey! I, Kees Fu, have grown up in this desert since I was a child, and I don't know how many years have passed.

He thought about the past, and became refreshed and proud, so the two lives continued on their way......;

Sarala - a layer of sand was rolled up, luckily it was still a step late, and he almost buried himself, but Kees Fu's eyes were already covered with a lot of fine sand, he held his breath, and simply stopped his steps, put down the bag of dry food and the whip in his hand, bent his head down, and only cared about stripping off the sleeve of his left hand, and skillfully stretched out his finger to wipe his eyelids for a while, then stepped up his pace, rushed to the front of the camel, grabbed the rope, and walked slowly.

The storm was still howling, and the desert waves were rising and falling even more violently. The old, useless animal was panting and could barely move forward, so its body softened and it dropped its front hooves, looked at Kees Fu, raised its head, and kept pouring out a lot of food from its food bag, its upper teeth tilted against its lower jaw, as if chewing casually.

After licking for a while, it still didn't move on, and Kees Fu seemed to be impatient.

"Old beast! Get up......"

He wanted to raise his whip to strike, but seeing the bags of heavy objects on its back, and its walking unsteadily with difficulty, he seemed to soften automatically with some reluctance.

Oh! Can't embarrass it! Eight or ten years ago, it was so helpful, and earned me a lot of money. The upper tribe borrowed it to help with logistics work to defend against enemy soldiers, eh! Don't despise it, it has also been to the front line. When it came back from the front, everyone said it was good, and could rush forward all day long without resting. But it's been three years! It's useless now. If it goes to the front line again, I'm afraid it won't be as energetic as before, and maybe it will be sent into the hands of the soldiers. No, I won't let it go...... No...... No......"

Kees Fu became kind, and showed a face of harmony. He expressed sympathy to the old travel companion, muttering to himself while shaking his head, loosening the rope in his hand, and tidying up the goods and luggage.

The gloomy sky never clears, and there is no sign of habitation all around. Travelers and livestock are hurrying on their way........

Sarala - the storm is still howling, and the desert leaves a track like a long snake, sending off two travelers in the desert........

Drama 248

Thunder and Lightning Drama Society

Jiaotong (1300) 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM

Leader: Chen Tu

Performers:

Bai Jiaotou & Lin Fei

Shan Jun...... Anna

Landlady...... Chen Jie

Maid...... Ying

Mrs. Zhang...... Jin Yi

Zhang Shengchang...... Ma Ling

Doctor...... Yi

Synopsis:

Shan Jun - a young widow whose husband was a revolutionary worker, but he is now dead! However, he left her a lot of money, so she lives a very comfortable life in Shanghai!

Her husband's friend Professor Bai now comes to her house every day to talk to her. What does he talk about? Every day, he tells her "...... Shan Jun, fly! Open up to the new territory!" Of course, he is desperately pursuing Shan Jun, but Shan Jun is not moved at all.

Suddenly, Mrs. Zhang Shengchang, a magazine editor and bookseller, runs here to discuss with Shan Jun, begging her to pity her for having three children and not to love her husband Shengchang. At that time, Shan Jun is both angry and amused, really inexplicable, because she has never loved Zhang Shengchang, and absolutely will not fall in love with Zhang Shengchang. After she tells Mrs. Zhang, Mrs. Zhang is relieved and goes back!

She doesn't love Professor Bai, and she will never love Zhang Shengchang, so who has Shan Jun fallen in love with? Let me tell you! She has fallen in love with the novelist Tang Huashi upstairs.

Tang Huashi is a novelist who writes novels for one and a half cents per thousand words. Unfortunately, he doesn't know anyone in the literary world, except for Zhang Shengchang, because he has just returned from Japan. But you must know that Zhang Shengchang is a man-eating, blood-sucking demon. Of course, the manuscript fees Tang Huashi gets are not enough to eat, let alone buy cigarettes!

Finally, before Tang Huashi finished writing his last manuscript, "How Should We Die," the poison he had taken took effect and he died!

Shan Jun? The blood of the person she sympathized with and fell in love with has now been sucked dry!

For the detailed twists and turns of the plot, please listen on the radio!

Ballad Singing 251

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Contentment in Poverty"

Coarse rice vegetables, stir-fried with white salt, are only enough to fill the belly. If you seek extravagance and greed for delicacies, there will be all kinds of mountain and sea delicacies. Ragged clothes are priceless and practical, patched up and patched up year after year. Thinking of filling boxes and cabinets for others to store, how can you have everything to wear until old age? Although it is only, a hard wooden bed with soft grass, I find it carefree and happy. Brocade quilts and embroidered bedding cannot sleep, tossing and turning until dawn. Old houses, just sweep, and repair them in time so they don't collapse. A thatched roof that doesn't leak is better than a tiled roof, with clear breeze and bright moon without restraint. People in the world don't know the happiness of contentment in poverty, busy and bustling all day long, working east and west for fame and fortune, for whom are you toiling and for whom are you busy? Try to see how many great rich people, are they still all well today? Isn't it a lifetime of empty labor.

Xing Ruiting's Three Smiles

Shanghai (1100) 4:00 PM to 4:45 PM

Opening "Dog Racing Track"

Shanghai is the number one prosperous place. There is dog racing all night long. How many young and wealthy children spend thousands of gold to buy dogs and compete with each other. They rely on their dog slaves to train them to be strong and healthy, and they can perform on the track. When they are temporarily locked in the cage, they only ask the dogs to bark Wang Wang. I only see the horses and dragons and the water and the people. They are like buying tickets and competing to dig up five oceans. One, four, two, three depend on the guests to pick. Greedily, they throw everything away and leave empty bags. Suddenly, they hear the bell ringing, and the group of people looks at the enclosure. The electric rabbit tries to run around, and the cage door opens and the dogs enter the track. Only to see that the rabbit is first and the dogs are behind, the machine starts quickly, and the dogs gallop without giving up. What is most hateful is that they suddenly fight and bite each other halfway, and there is no hope of winning, so the dogs stagger. The championship is won by others, and some people sit aside disheartened, with all the banknotes in their pockets lost.

Movie News

About "The Story of Louis Pasteur" 253

A Great Man on the Silver Screen Plays a Great Man in the World of Science

When "The Story of Louis Pasteur" was being filmed, an old-fashioned barber's chair suddenly appeared in the bedroom of Paul Muni, the lead actor in the film. The movie star was not using the chair as a sleeping device; he was using it for makeup purposes because the real Paul Muni was not like Pasteur in the film. His hair was shorter, his face was thinner, and he had no beard. Therefore, every morning, he had to spend at least two hours putting on makeup, turning himself into a Pasteur who was indistinguishable from the real Pasteur, before he could go to the set to work. The film details the life of Louis Pasteur, the great man in the scientific world and the benefactor of all mankind. He fearlessly defied the wrath of the king and the cold ridicule of the great gentlemen, boldly pierced the veil of life and death, and declared war on the invisible public enemy of mankind. For the happiness of Parisian women and the happiness of all mankind, he desperately fought against those invisible murderous demons. These bad things had gradually invaded the beautiful French women from the sewers of Paris. It is said that the film has passed the censorship notice and will soon be released at the Grand Theater.

News of the Establishment of the First Branch of Chongsheng 256

The new song and opera organization in this city—Chongsheng Society, has been established for less than a month. Due to the soundness of the organization, the number of people registering to join is exceptionally enthusiastic, so the society's affairs are thriving. The society originally planned to hold its first performance at the end of March, but it was delayed for a long time due to a request from a certain National Arts Research Society to perform at its one-week anniversary celebration.

Now, in order to facilitate the participation of young people in the central district who love opera art, it has been specially agreed with the authorities of the American School Entrance Examination at No. 45, Hele Lane, at the intersection of Xinzha Road and Parker Road, to provide assistance in establishing the first branch in the school. Mr. Xin Zijun, a member of the society, will serve as the director of the branch, in charge of recruiting members and carrying out affairs for the branch, starting today.

Men and women comrades who love opera art are welcome to join. Brochures are available upon request.

In addition, the society is preparing to publish a "Chongsheng" type of daily newspaper, which was published on the 22nd. The contents include Mr. Fei Si's "The Inevitability of the Emergence of 'National Defense Drama'," Mr. Liu Yawei's "The So-Called Chinese Radio Drama," and news of the regular performances of "Roar, China," etc. It is available at all newsstands for two copper coins per copy.
